## Recent changes
_Append one dated bullet per shipped, UI-visible change. Newest first._

- **2026-06-20 (branch `claude/festive-booth-75dabe`, UAT only тАФ NOT deployed) тАФ Call log: AI bullet summary + smart pre-fill + KVA/Rechnung Open Actions (our-AI-over-transcript).** New **`calls.enrichment`** JSONB (migration **0077**, applied) holds one LLM pass over the transcript тЖТ `summary_bullets[]` + `intent{wants_kva,wants_invoice,wants_appointment}` + `prefill{service_description,address,problem,preferred_time}`. Service [call_enrichment.py](backend/app/services/call_enrichment.py) (best-effort, no-op without `OPENAI_API_KEY`, model=`gpt-4o-mini`); runs at post-call ingest ([post_call.py](backend/app/services/post_call.py)) and lazily back-fills on detail open ([calls.py](backend/app/api/routes/calls.py) `_detail`). **(1) Bullet summary:** the drawer's Kiki-Zusammenfassung renders `summary_bullets` as a list (falls back to the ElevenLabs paragraph) тАФ [LogDrawer.tsx](frontend/src/pages/calls/log/LogDrawer.tsx), type on [shared.ts](frontend/src/pages/calls/shared.ts) `CallEnrichment`. **(2) Smart pre-fill:** create-forms read `?call_id=` and pre-fill subject + first line-item (KVA [CostEstimateFormPage.tsx](frontend/src/pages/CostEstimateFormPage.tsx), Rechnung [InvoiceFormPage.tsx](frontend/src/pages/InvoiceFormPage.tsx)) and the appointment modal surfaces address/problem/`preferred_time` ([Modals.tsx](frontend/src/pages/calls/Modals.tsx)); drawer `goKva`/`goInvoice` now pass `call_id`. тЪая╕П The AI extracts *descriptive* fields only тАФ **no prices/line-item amounts** (those stay 0 for the user). **(3) Open Actions parity:** new backend kinds in [actions.py](backend/app/api/routes/actions.py) тАФ `kva_suggested`/`invoice_suggested` (fire from enrichment intent when no KVA/invoice exists yet for the Vorgang; `call_id` set so they deep-link) + `invoice_to_send`/`invoice_pending_payment` (mirror the KVA lifecycle). Drawer shows "Kostenvoranschlag/Rechnung erw├дhnt" cards (one-click тЖТ pre-filled form); Posteingang/hero render them as decision cards that **navigate** on primary (new `DecisionVM.route` in [posteingang/api.ts](frontend/src/pages/posteingang/api.ts), wired in [PosteingangPage.tsx](frontend/src/pages/PosteingangPage.tsx) + [DashboardPage.tsx](frontend/src/pages/DashboardPage.tsx)); labels/tones in [shared.ts](frontend/src/pages/calls/shared.ts) + [Inbox.tsx](frontend/src/pages/calls/Inbox.tsx). `tsc -b` green; backend 49/49 on the touched suites (fake client gained `.filter`/`.limit`). **Preview-verified in kiki-test-007** (login kikitest01@gmail.com): seeded 2 calls with KVA/Rechnung intent тЖТ drawer bullets (3) + KVA card render, "KVA erstellen" opens the form pre-filled (Kunde + ANF- + Betreff "Heizung entl├╝ften" + position), Posteingang shows "Kostenvoranschlag/Rechnung f├╝r тАж?" + invoice send/payment actions (10 decisions). NOTE: kiki-test-007 has leftover seeded intent on 2 calls (reversible test data).

- **2026-06-19 (branch `claude/adoring-golick-77f9d5`, UAT only тАФ committed, NOT deployed) тАФ EMPLOYEE PORTAL: personal identity + per-employee data scoping + technician-dispatch fixes.** Four batches. **(1) Identity/display:** the employee Dashboard greeting + sidebar badge now show the PERSON (their `full_name` from the `['me']` cache; first name in the greeting), never the company; the admin login still shows the company name. The sidebar read stale `session.user_metadata` тЖТ now reads the primed `['me']` cache (and `PATCH /api/users/me` also syncs Supabase auth `user_metadata`; the settings modal invalidates `['me']`) so a name edit shows instantly. White-label footer drops the company email (keeps the name). Files: `DashboardPage`, `Sidebar`, `AppLayout`, `PersonalSettingsModal`, `users.py`. **(2) Per-employee scoping (core):** new `backend/app/services/scope.py` тАФ `resolve_scope(client, user)` walks the assignment graph ONCE (admins short-circuit тЖТ unrestricted; a plain `employee` тЖТ only their own work: cases they're on via `case_employees` тИк their assigned inquiries' cases, plus those cases' inquiries/calls/appointments/customers, plus calls forward-linked by `inquiry_id`). `EmployeeScope.filter_{cases,inquiries,calls,appointments,customers}(q)` are no-ops for admins. Wired into ALL five dashboards (`dashboard.py` overview/anrufe/finanzen/ki-nutzung/ai-insights тАФ finances best-effort by `case_id`; helpers keep `org_id` + an optional `scope=None` so the existing unit tests still call them with a bare org_id), the actions worklist (`actions.py` `_aggregate(org_id, scope)` + scoped `/api/actions/pending` тЖТ hero + Posteingang), `GET /api/cases`, and `GET /api/calls`. **Verified live vs kiki-test-007:** admin sees 34 cases / 52 calls; a real employee is scoped to 3 cases / 7 calls / 1 action (employee тЙд admin everywhere). Hero deck + Posteingang reframed for employees as **тАЮMeine Aufgaben"/тАЮAufgaben"** (admin keeps тАЮPosteingang"/тАЮEntscheidungen"). **(3) Admin ticket-load:** `GET /api/employees` now returns `open_tickets` (count of OPEN F├дlle per employee via `case_employees тиЭ cases`); the case тАЮMitarbeiter" assignment picker shows a colour-graded **тАЮN offen"** badge so an admin avoids overloading one person. **(4) Technician dispatch:** Calendar dispatch selector lists TECHNICIANS only (`is_technician`), not all employees; the case-card send-order is gated to **confirmed** appointments only (`confirmedAppts`); a per-job **тАЮErneut senden"** button appears once a link is dispatched (disabled after the report is submitted); a reschedule/edit of the appointment time **auto-resends** the updated job link to the assigned technician (`_maybe_resend_technician_link` in `appointments.py`, only if previously dispatched); **photo upload fixed** тАФ the strict `startswith("image/")` check rejected phone uploads with empty/octet-stream/HEIC content-types тЖТ now falls back to the file extension (`technician_jobs.add_photo`), and `apiUpload` surfaces the backend's German error verbatim. Backend suite **737/0**; `tsc -b --force` + `vite build` green; live `/openapi.json` route-check + 401 auth-gate OK. **Config decisions (Amber):** finances/AI scoped (not hidden); technician link gated in the case card (not moved out); employee tasks = the existing hero тЖТ Posteingang to-do, personalized. **Follow-ups (not done):** preview-MCP visual render of the employee portal needs a real employee login session (no anon key in this env тЖТ verified at the data layer instead); auto-resend triggers on `scheduled_at` change only (not pure notes/address edits).

- **2026-06-18 (branch `claude/festive-booth-75dabe`, UAT only тАФ NOT deployed) тАФ Call log screen: Luca's 5 requested tweaks.** All frontend-only (no backend/migration changes; status edit reuses the existing `PATCH /api/inquiries/{id}` which already accepts `status`). (1) **New Status column** in the `/calls` table ([LogTable.tsx](frontend/src/pages/calls/log/LogTable.tsx)), at **position 2** (Richtung ┬╖ **Status** ┬╖ Zust├дndig ┬╖ тАж), rendering the **full German label** via `StatusPill` (Offen / In Bearbeitung / Erledigt; `тАФ` when the call has no Vorgang). Shows the linked **inquiry status** (`inquiry_status`). (2) **Emergency no longer hides the subject** тАФ added `iconOnly` to `NotdienstBadge` ([atoms.tsx](frontend/src/pages/calls/atoms.tsx)); the Betreff cell now shows a compact 20px pulsing red triangle (tooltip тАЮNotdienst") at the *start* of the cell instead of the wide тАЮЁЯЪи Notdienst" word-badge, so the subject text stays readable. (3) **Status editable from the drawer** тАФ new `StatusSelect` radix dropdown ([atoms.tsx](frontend/src/pages/calls/atoms.tsx)) placed FIRST in the drawer's Aktionen row ([LogDrawer.tsx](frontend/src/pages/calls/log/LogDrawer.tsx)), shown when the call has an `inquiry_id`; picking Offen/In Bearbeitung/Erledigt fires `PATCH /api/inquiries/{id}` `{status}` + toast + cache refresh (the table column reflects it). (4) **Duration & time wording** тАФ new `fmtDurationLong` in [shared.ts](frontend/src/pages/calls/shared.ts) (column now reads тАЮ3 Min 6 Sek" / тАЮ33 Sek" instead of тАЮ3:06") and new `fmtClockUhr` in [datetime.ts](frontend/src/lib/datetime.ts) (Uhrzeit column now тАЮ17:29 Uhr"). (5) **Responsive gap fix** тАФ added a trailing `w-full` filler `<th>`/`<td>` to the table so on wide displays the real columns pack left at natural widths and the spacer absorbs the slack (no more inter-column white space); table `min-w` 940тЖТ1040, day-divider colSpan 8тЖТ10. `tsc -b` green; **preview-MCP verified** with TobiasDachdecker's 33 real calls (Status pills, тАЮтАж Min тАж Sek"/тАЮUhr" wording, drawer status dropdown opens with all 3 options, 2200px-wide no-gap layout, and emergency icon + visible subject via an intercepted-response flag). UAT login: `govindyadav0703@gmail.com` / `test@admin123`.

Juni"` via new `fmtDayDate()` in `log/util.ts`) ┬╖ **Uhrzeit** ┬╖ **Dauer**. Whole row opens the existing `LogDrawer` (unchanged); Fall/Anfrage + Projekt chips are separate click targets. Table is in an `overflow-x-auto` wrapper with `min-w-[940px]` so all columns survive on narrow screens; sticky `<thead>`. Triage (assign existing / new Vorgang / spam) + Fall/Projekt link kept.
  - **z-layering fix (important):** `LogDrawer` is `z-30` тАФ ABOVE Topbar (`z-10`) / sidebar (`z-20`), BELOW the popup layer (shared `Modal` `z-50`, `AssignDropdown` `z-70`). - **2026-06-10 (branch `fix/reported-bugs-magiclink-confirm-dupphone`, LOCAL/UAT, NOT deployed) тАФ bug #3 reschedule-duplicate fixed (admin-gated proposal + safety timer).** A reschedule never creates a second appointment: the agent (`change_appointment`) stamps the customer's requested slot onto the EXISTING row (`customer_proposed_*`) тАФ no new row, no call/email sent тАФ and the admin commits it (`approve-proposal` = in-place move + confirmation; `decline-proposal` = clear, and if the customer abandoned the old slot it cancels + notifies). New: agent asks the date when the customer has several upcoming appointments (precise link); captures `replace_original` intent; a per-org safety timer (`agent_configs.reschedule_request_timeout_hours`, default 24, set in Kiki-Zentrale тЖТ Autonomie тЖТ Termine) bounds the pending request. **Timer action is gated by appointments autonomy level** (reuses `appointments_level`): L1/L2 тЖТ only flag overdue in the UI (never auto-cancel a real booking); L3 тЖТ auto-resolve (drop the proposal; if replace-intent, cancel the slot + notify). Timer runs in the existing outbound sweep (`run_due_reschedule_expiry` in `outbound_dispatch`, best-effort so it can't break the reminder sweep) тАФ no new infra. Migration **0063** (additive: `reschedule_expires_at`, `reschedule_replace_intent` on appointments; `reschedule_request_timeout_hours` on agent_configs) applied to prod DB. Verified: migration columns in DB, `tsc -b` clean, 18 appointment-route tests (incl. new decline-replace-intent test), Kiki-Zentrale timer input render-proven (L2 shows "├╝berf├дllig markiert", L3 shows "automatisch aufgel├╢st"). тЪая╕П Backend can't force the voice agent to pick "reschedule" over "new booking" тАФ that's the ElevenLabs agent prompt/tool wording (small separate item); the backend now guarantees no duplicate row once a reschedule is recorded as a proposal.

- **2026-06-09 (ЁЯЪА DEPLOYED to prod тАФ `main` `22a5e89`) тАФ fixed the spiky `/api/customers?limit=500` 500s. Backend `d4165668` SUCCESS.** Root cause: the shared sync Supabase client fans out concurrent `run_in_threadpool` queries over ONE HTTP/2 connection тЖТ `httpx.RemoteProtocolError: ConnectionTerminated` (intermittent, hits every fan-out page). Fix: forced PostgREST to **HTTP/1.1** (connection pool, one conn per concurrent request) in `db/supabase_client.py`. Verified 40/40 concurrent тЖТ 200 on prod. (The earlier CORS-on-error fix just made this previously CORS-masked 500 visible.) Also backfilled `cancelled_at` for the test org's pre-fix cancellations so they surface as "Termin storniert" actions (user-approved).

- **2026-06-09 (ЁЯЪА DEPLOYED to prod тАФ `main` `45314b8`) тАФ ROOT-CAUSED + fixed the real "page crashes / cannot be reloaded" bug (it was NOT chunk-skew). Frontend deploy `159f8d5e` SUCCESS + backend `0133dcf2` SUCCESS (priors REMOVED; both verified via `deployment list`, not just CLI "complete"). Validated locally before deploy тЖТ no crash this time.**
  - **The crash = browser auto-translation.** `index.html` shipped `<html lang="en">` on a **German-only** app with no translate opt-out, so Chrome/Google Translate rewrote text nodes out from under React тЖТ `NotFoundError: Failed to execute 'insertBefore' on 'Node'` (the page break, on pages with NO code involvement тАФ KVA form, cancelled-appointment route). Fix: `<html lang="de" translate="no">` + `<meta name="google" content="notranslate">`. тЪая╕П **Side effect:** browser auto-translate is now disabled (correct тАФ app is German-only by design; auto-translating crashed it). Verified live: prod serves `<html lang="de" translate="no">`.
  - **The intermittent CORS/500s were transient deploy-restart artifacts** (user tested seconds after a backend redeploy). Verified `/api/customers?limit=500` returns 200 **with** the `Access-Control-Allow-Origin` header. Hardened anyway: new http middleware (INNER to `CORSMiddleware`) returns a JSON 500 so unhandled errors flow back through CORS and carry the header тАФ a bare Starlette `ServerErrorMiddleware` 500 lacks it, which is why a transient 500 showed as "blocked by CORS policy". +`test_cors_on_error`.
  - тЪая╕П **The earlier "chunk-skew" hypothesis was wrong** тАФ the `serve.json` no-cache/immutable headers are still a good practice (and live), but they were NOT the crash cause. The crash was translation. Don't re-attribute.

Hotfix `dc42136` stripped `serve.json` to the valid `headers`-only config; redeploy `65ea8290` SUCCESS. **Lesson reaffirmed:** always verify `railway deployment list` (CRASHED vs SUCCESS) тАФ the `--ci` "Deploy complete"/exit-0 did NOT mean healthy. Also: `frontend/public/serve.json` must stay pure serve-handler config (no comments/$schema).

- **2026-06-08 (Architecture & performance hardening тАФ from `ARCHITECTURE_AUDIT_2026-06-08.md`; branch `fix/arch-audit-hardening-2026-06-08`; LOCAL/UAT, NOT deployed) тАФ fixes the correctness/security/leak findings from the multi-agent audit. Backend tests 536 pass / 6 PRE-EXISTING reds (unchanged baseline); frontend `tsc -b` clean; vitest 16 pass / 5 PRE-EXISTING reds (RufumleitungGuidePage).**
  - **P0 correctness / data-integrity (backend):** CSV-import dedup now PAGES past PostgREST's silent 1000-row cap (`csv_import.py` + `gen_customer_number`) тАФ re-importing on an org >1000 customers no longer creates duplicates; same paging applied to the unbounded count/revenue/timeline reads (`customers._list` enrichment, `projects._list`, `dashboard._fetch_calls`/`_finanzen`, `build_customer_timeline`) so large orgs stop silently under-counting. Multi-write **atomicity**: `book_appointment` (inquiryтЖТappointment) and `invoices._create` (invoiceтЖТKVA back-link) now compensate (delete the orphan) on a failed 2nd write. `post_call` L3 auto-confirm is now **idempotent** (conditional `update тАж where status='pending'` + gate notify on the returned row) тЖТ no duplicate real-customer confirmation calls/emails on overlapping webhook deliveries.
  - **P0 security:** removed the `master_webhook_secret="change-me"` fallback (now empty = fail-closed) + `validate_runtime_config()` aborts boot in `APP_ENV=production` when it (or DB creds) is unset; **FK-in-org** validation added to `projects._create` + `invoices._create` (service-role bypasses RLS тЖТ was an IDOR vector); JWKS cache TTL 1hтЖТconfigurable 300s (`JWKS_TTL_SECONDS`).
  - **P1 parallelism / perf:** new `services/common.fetch_all_rows` (paging) + `run_parallel` (private threadpool тАФ keeps the sync helpers sync so the direct-call unit tests stay green, no AnyIO starvation). Independent fan-out reads now run concurrently in `customers._detail`, `projects._list`, `employees._list`, `cost_estimates._list`, `dashboard._finanzen`, and both call timelines. `conversation_init` + `deps.get_current_user` no longer block the event loop (run_in_threadpool). `mark-read` 3 queries тЖТ 1 (common case). ElevenLabs tool-ID cache got a 1h TTL (was never re-fetched тЖТ stale ids forever). Outbound-dispatch occasion email is now 5s-bounded so a slow provider can't serialize the LIVE sweep. `calls` list `limit/offset` bounded.
  - **Frontend (UI-visible тАФ responsiveness/leaks/padding):** Sidebar is now a **mobile drawer** (`md=768px`: backdrop + Escape + route-change close; static rail on desktop) with a Topbar hamburger; data tables (Kunden, KVAs) hide non-essential columns under `md`; Modal/Copilot-widget/profile-dropdown/CommandPalette sized to stay inside small viewports; overflow "leaks" fixed (`truncate`/`min-w-0` on call rows + workspace pane, Tag wraps on mobile); padding scale unified (Topbar/page/footer/hero). Re-render fixes: `useMemo` on Theme + AdminAuth context values. Leak fixes: shared `useToast` hook (effect-owned timer, replaces 7 uncleaned `setTimeout`s), idempotent OAuth-popup listener cleanup, `useMe()` de-dup. тЪая╕П **Live preview render-proof at 375/768/1280 NOT yet done** (per the UI-done convention) тАФ recommended before any prod deploy; Amber to verify manually.
  - **Deferred (documented in the audit, NOT bugs тАФ too risky for a pre-prod window):** god-file тЖТ service-layer extraction; durable job queue for BackgroundTasks; full optimistic-update rollout; broad bare-except typing sweep. Tracked as P2/P3 in `ARCHITECTURE_AUDIT_2026-06-08.md`.

  - **Backend reliability (takes effect on uvicorn restart):** `dashboard.overview` was an `async def` calling the SYNC Supabase client directly тЖТ it blocked the event loop on ~8 serial HTTP calls, stalling the **whole worker** for every other concurrent user (the "falls over under load" cause the perf doc missed). Now offloaded + parallelized via `asyncio.gather(run_in_threadpool(...))` (non-blocking, ~1 round-trip). `customers._list` made async + parallelized (page query + 5 type-counts concurrent, then 3 enrichment counts concurrent) тЖТ ~11 serial round-trips тЖТ ~2 wall-clock; kept `count="exact"` (avoids PostgREST's 1000-row cap). A sweep confirmed dashboard was the ONLY blocking handler. `dashboard.py`, `customers.py`.
  - **Frontend smoothness:** optimistic call-delete (`onMutate` removes the row from `['calls']` instantly, rollback on error, reconcile on settle) тАФ fixes the delete lag AND the "stuck on the transcript" race (auto-select now picks the correct next call from a list that no longer contains the deleted one); global React Query `staleTime: 30s` (no refetch-on-navigation); 21 route pages code-split via `React.lazy` + `Suspense` (smaller initial bundle / faster first paint). `CallDetail.tsx`, `main.tsx`, `App.tsx`.

- **2026-05-28 тАФ Agent-logic fix (backend, not UI): returning customers re-asked for their address.** On a repeat inbound call, `hk_identifyCustomer` returned `address: null` for an already-registered customer, so the agent (correctly, per prompt) re-collected the address. **Root cause:** `identify.py` carried a STALE private copy of `_format_address` that only parsed the `{street,city,postal_code}`/plain-string shapes тАФ it had no `raw` branch, so it silently dropped every `{"raw": "..."}` address (the shape `get_or_create_customer`, `updateCustomerData`, and the CRM admin `_addr` all actually write). Added parametrized regression test (`test_identify_returns_stored_customer_fields`, covers raw/structured/string shapes) тАФ 143 hermetic tests pass (`-m "not live"`); test customer cleaned up. - **2026-05-28 тАФ Wave 3 / Agent 3.2: unified `GET /api/calls/{id}/timeline` endpoint + vertical Verlauf-tab redesign (commit `bb00e5e`).** Replaces the customer-scoped Inquiries/Termine/KVA-accordion that the Verlauf tab used to render with a true call-scoped vertical timeline. **3.2.A тАФ Backend** (`backend/app/api/routes/calls.py`): new `GET /api/calls/{id}/timeline` route + `_build_timeline(org_id, call_id)` helper. Aggregates 8 event kinds from existing columns тАФ no new migration, no new `events` table. **Sources:** (1) `call_created` from `calls.started_at` (or `created_at` fallback); (2) `inquiry_status_changed` from `inquiries.updated_at` ONLY when `status != 'open'` (open = no transition yet, no event); (3) `appointment_confirmed` / `appointment_rejected` / `alternative_proposed` from `appointments.confirmed_at` / `rejected_at` / `alternative_proposed_at` (Wave 2.4's migration 0026 columns); (4) `kva_sent` / `kva_accepted` / `kva_rejected` from `cost_estimates.sent_at` / `accepted_at` / `rejected_at`. Each event carries `{id, kind, timestamp, actor_kind, actor_name, description, entity_id, extras}` тАФ id is composed as `<entity>:<uuid>:<sub-event>` (e.g. `appointment:appt-1:confirmed`) so the React `key` is stable across re-renders. Actor inference is heuristic (no per-row "who changed it" audit column exists today): `call_created` тЖТ `actor_kind='kiki'`; `inquiry_status_changed` to in_progress/completed тЖТ `actor_kind='employee'`; appointment lifecycle events тЖТ `actor_kind='employee'`; KVA accept/reject тЖТ `actor_kind='system' actor_name='Kunde'` (the customer's decision); KVA sent тЖТ `actor_kind='employee'`. Sort: newest-first by ISO timestamp (`sort(key=lambda e: e['timestamp'], reverse=True)` тАФ ISO strings sort lexicographically). **Tenant isolation:** every SELECT chains `.eq('org_id', org_id)`; cross-org call_id never matches the initial `calls` SELECT so `_build_timeline` returns `None` and the route translates to 404 before any aggregation runs (no info leak about other tenants' inquiry/appointment IDs). **assignment_changed event kind is reserved in the literal type but NOT surfaced in v1** тАФ `inquiries.assigned_to` / `inquiries.assigned_employee_id` are overwritten in place with no audit row, so we'd have to invent history we don't have. Flagged as a follow-up that needs either an `agent_writes_audit`-style table for assignments OR widening the existing audit table's scope. **3.2.B тАФ Frontend** (`frontend/src/pages/CallLogsPage.tsx`): `VerlaufTab({customerId})` becomes `VerlaufTab({callId})` тАФ the prop type and the call site `{tab === 'course' && <VerlaufTab callId={call.id} />}` flip together. Inside, replaced the 3-section accordion (Durchgef├╝hrte Aktionen / Termine / KVAs) with a single vertical `<ol>` rendered inside a `relative pl-5` wrapper. **Visual:** 1px `bg-border` rail at `left-[7px]` running top to bottom; each event is an `<li className="relative">` with a 10px dot pinned at `-left-[18px]` (so it sits dead-centre on the 7px rail) with a 2px `ring-surface` ring so the dot reads cleanly above the rail. Each row has a meta row (relative time + actor chip) and a description line below. **Dot color map** (`TIMELINE_KIND_DOT`): call_created=blue-500 ┬╖ inquiry_status_changed=muted ┬╖ appointment_confirmed=green-primary ┬╖ appointment_rejected=red-500 ┬╖ alternative_proposed=amber-500 ┬╖ kva_sent/accepted/rejected=purple-500/600/400 ┬╖ assignment_changed=cyan-500 (reserved). **Actor chip** (`ACTOR_CHIP`): kiki=green-tint-50/green-deep ┬╖ employee=blue-100/blue-800 ┬╖ system=alt/faint тАФ distinct visual lane per source so a scan groups "Kiki did X" rows apart from "Mitarbeiter did Y". **Relative-time formatter** (`relativeTimeDe`): "gerade eben" / "vor N Min" / "vor N Std" / "vor N Tagen" up to 7 days, then falls back to absolute short date (`28. Mai 2026`). Absolute timestamp on hover via `<time title={absoluteTimeDe(...)}>`. Empty state: simple `<p className="text-sm text-muted">Keine Verlaufs-Eintr├дge.</p>` (no card frame). Loading state: "Lade Verlauf тАж". **Tab structure preserved** тАФ the three tabs (Aktionen / Details / Verlauf) and the tab bar UI are untouched; only the CONTENT inside `tab === 'course'` changed. **3.2.C тАФ Code-tidy drive-by**: removed the now-unused `CustomerDetail` interface, `statusDot` helper, and `Euro` lucide import from the same file (they were only referenced by the old VerlaufTab body). Section / Tag / fmtTime / STATUS_TAG remain тАФ still used by ActionsTab + DetailsTab. **Tests:** new `backend/tests/test_call_timeline.py` with **8 hermetic tests**: (1) cross-org call_id returns None (route тЖТ 404); (2) every per-table SELECT carries `.eq('org_id', ORG)` тАФ recording `_FakeClient` asserts at least 4 org_id filters fire when inquiries/appointments/cost_estimates all have data; (3) `call_created` event always emitted, even on a brand-new call with no inquiries; (4) `status='open'` does NOT emit `inquiry_status_changed` (no transition has happened); (5) `status='completed'` emits the event with `actor_kind='employee'`, German label "Erledigt", extras carrying title + status; (6) all 3 appointment lifecycle events fire (confirmed / rejected with reason in extras / alternative_proposed); (7) all 3 KVA events fire with number flowing into extras, accept/reject get `actor_kind='system' actor_name='Kunde'`; (8) final list is strictly descending by ISO timestamp across all kinds, newest event (1h ago inquiry flip) at index 0, oldest (call_created 5 days ago) at the tail. Backend `pytest -q -m "not live"` = **137 passing, 6 deselected** (was 129; +8 mine; if Agent 3.1's mini-calendar +3 land separately, the total will roll up to 140). Frontend `npm run build` clean. **Wins preserved**: lazy audio loading + "Aufnahme laden" button untouched ┬╖ clean centre conversation panel untouched ┬╖ light Bot/User speaker icons untouched ┬╖ three-tab right-panel structure (Aktionen / Details / Verlauf) untouched ┬╖ list-card enrichment (Wave 2.1) untouched ┬╖ Anfragen/Aktionen tab switcher (Wave 2.2) untouched ┬╖ right-panel polish (Wave 2.3) untouched ┬╖ appointment card + mini-calendar slot (Wave 2.4 / 3.1) untouched. **Coordination with parallel Agent 3.1**: their `AppointmentCard.tsx` + `MiniCalendar.tsx` + `appointments.py` / `test_appointments_actions.py` work is in a different file set; my changes are confined to `calls.py` + the VerlaufTab function body + a new test file. No overlap, no merge conflict. **Deferred follow-ups:** (1) **`assignment_changed` event** тАФ `inquiries.assigned_to` / `assigned_employee_id` is overwritten in place; the event kind exists in the TS literal type + the color-map but the backend never emits it. Surfacing this needs either (a) a new `inquiry_assignments_history` table written-to on every assign mutation, or (b) extending the existing `agent_writes_audit` scope to cover human assignments (currently agent-only). Either is its own change. (2) **Per-row "who changed it" actor names** тАФ currently the actor for `inquiry_status_changed` and the appointment lifecycle events is the generic string "Mitarbeiter", because we don't store which specific user clicked the button. Adding `confirmed_by_user_id` / `rejected_by_user_id` columns to `appointments` (and similar for inquiries) would let us join through `users.full_name` and surface a real name. (3) **Realtime updates** тАФ the timeline currently fetches once on tab open via TanStack `useQuery` with default staleness; if a sibling user confirms an appointment while this tab is open, the user has to switch tabs and back to see the new event. A Supabase Realtime channel on the relevant tables тЖТ cache invalidation would close that. (4) **Customer-name on KVA actor_name** тАФ `kva_accepted` / `kva_rejected` currently say "Kunde" generically; resolving via the linked `customer_id` would let us say e.g. "Max Mustermann" instead. Minor enhancement. Per the local-UAT-Railway-prod-on-approval standing rule: committed + pushed to `origin/main`; **no `railway up`**. Backend uvicorn needs a manual restart to pick up the new `/api/calls/{id}/timeline` route (no `--reload`).

- **2026-05-28 тАФ Wave 3 / Agent 3.1: compact 7-day mini-calendar inside `AppointmentCard` + new `/api/appointments/calendar` busy-slot endpoint.** Slots into the TODO marker left by Agent 2.4 (commit `9e7df01`) тАФ replaces a HTML placeholder with a live 7-day grid that paints the proposed appointment + internal conflicts and lets the user click an empty cell to seed the Alternative-vorschlagen flow. **3.1.A тАФ Backend `GET /api/appointments/calendar`** (`backend/app/api/routes/appointments.py`): new lightweight endpoint accepting `?from=YYYY-MM-DD&to=YYYY-MM-DD&self_id=...` and returning `[{id, start_time, end_time, status, is_self}, ...]`. Org-scoped via `require_org`; filters to `status IN ('pending', 'confirmed')` (cancelled/deleted aren't conflicts so they're dropped); derives `end_time` from `scheduled_at + duration_minutes` so the frontend doesn't have to recompute. `self_id` marks the currently-viewed appointment with `is_self=true` so the UI can render it as the highlighted green proposal rather than treating it as a conflict block. Deliberately kept separate from the existing heavier `GET /api/appointments` route (the latter pulls customer + employee join data the mini-calendar doesn't need, so paying that cost on every week shift would be wasteful). Re-used the appointments table's existing `org_id`/`scheduled_at` index pattern тАФ no new migration needed. **3.1.B тАФ New `MiniCalendar.tsx`** (`frontend/src/pages/calls/MiniCalendar.tsx`): standalone component, ~330 lines. Layout тАФ 7 day columns (36px each, total 252px + 24px hour-label gutter = 276px wide, fits inside the 320px right panel with `p-2` padding) ├Ч 14 hour rows (20px each = 280px tall, 06:00-20:00 grid). Day-label row above the grid shows `Mo Di Mi Do Fr Sa So` + the date number; today's column gets a `bg-green-tint-50/40` wash + `text-green-primary` label. **3.1.B.1 тАФ Coloring scheme**: proposed slot (the appointment being viewed, identified via `is_self=true` from backend OR via local `proposedStart`/`proposedEnd` props when not yet in the DB) = solid `bg-green-primary` block with white border and shadow. Internal conflicts colored by status: `status='confirmed'` = `bg-error/85` red block, `status='pending'` = `bg-warning/80` amber block. Blocks are absolute-positioned with `top = (start_hour - 6) * 20px` and `height = duration_minutes / 60 * 20px` (min 8px so a 15-min slot still has a visible bar). `pointer-events-none` on the blocks so the empty-cell click targets underneath still register. **3.1.B.2 тАФ Click-to-propose**: every empty hour cell is a `<button>` covering the 20px row; clicking fires `onProposeSlot(start: Date, end: Date)` with a 1-hour range starting at the clicked hour. Past cells get `disabled` + `cursor-not-allowed` + `bg-alt/30` so the user can't propose a slot the backend would 422 anyway (the `/propose-alternative` route already validates `start_time > now()`, so this is a UX echo of the backend rule, not a duplicate of the auth check). **3.1.B.3 тАФ Navigation**: `тЧА тЦ╢` lucide chevron buttons left/right of a centered window label (e.g. "28.тАУ3. Jun" when same-month, "28.05 тАУ 04.06" when crossing months). Each click shifts `weekStart` by ┬▒7 days; TanStack Query refetches automatically because the window dates are in the `queryKey`. The window is anchored on the proposed slot's Monday if it's in a future week (so the user lands on the right week immediately), otherwise on today's Monday. **3.1.B.4 тАФ Data fetching**: TanStack `useQuery` with `queryKey: ['mini-calendar', from, to, selfId]`, `staleTime: 60_000` (60s тАФ matches the right-panel polling cadence; the mini-calendar doesn't need second-level freshness, the user-driven mutations on the parent card invalidate the cache when needed). `URLSearchParams` builds the query string so `selfId` is omitted cleanly when null. **3.1.B.5 тАФ Legend**: 3 swatches below the grid (`Vorschlag` / `Best├дtigt` / `Ausstehend`) at `text-[9px]` size тАФ compact key so a new user can decode the color scheme without hunting through docs. **3.1.C тАФ `AppointmentCard.tsx` integration**: replaced the `{/* TODO: Agent 3.1 mini-calendar тАФ render <MiniCalendarSlot /> here once it's built. */}` comment marker (cleaned up the misnested `{/* {/*` typo on the same row while there) and added `<MiniCalendar>` between the alt-picker / lock-state UI and the action-buttons row тАФ `!altAlreadySent && <MiniCalendar ... />` so the calendar disappears once the appointment is locked into "Alternative gesendet" state (the user can't propose new times then anyway). Added `proposedEndIso` memo computing `scheduled_at + duration_minutes` (fallback 60min) and a `handleMiniCalendarPick` callback that calls `setAltStart(dateToDtLocal(start))` + `setAltEnd(dateToDtLocal(end))` + `setAltPickerOpen(true)` тАФ populates the existing date/time inputs and pops the picker open without auto-submitting (the user still clicks "Alternative senden" explicitly per spec). New `dateToDtLocal(d: Date)` helper extracted from the existing `isoToDtLocal` so both paths share the same `YYYY-MM-DDTHH:mm` formatter. **3.1.D тАФ Tests**: 3 new hermetic tests in `backend/tests/test_appointments_actions.py` (`test_calendar_busy_slots_returns_lightweight_shape` тАФ pending + confirmed both surface, end_time = start + duration_minutes; `test_calendar_marks_self_id_correctly` тАФ `self_id` matches stamp `is_self=true` on the right row and false elsewhere; `test_calendar_is_org_scoped` тАФ recording `_FakeClient` confirms `.eq('org_id', user.org_id)` runs on the SELECT chain). Backend `pytest -q -m "not live"` = **140 passing, 6 deselected** (was 137 immediately before this commit; +3 mine in `test_appointments_actions.py` going from 12 тЖТ 15 tests тАФ verified in isolation: `pytest tests/test_appointments_actions.py` тЖТ `15 passed`). Baseline rose well above the brief's expected 129 because Wave 2.2 (commit `96fadb3`, +8 tests) and Wave 3.2 (commit `5b45c6a`, +8 tests) both landed mid-Wave-3 between when the brief was written and when I shipped. Frontend `npm run build` clean (TS + Vite OK; pre-existing 1.7MB chunk-size warning is the unrelated app-wide concern that's been flagged in previous bullets тАФ not introduced here). **Wins preserved**: lazy audio loading + "Aufnahme laden" untouched ┬╖ clean centre conversation panel untouched ┬╖ light Bot/User speaker icons untouched ┬╖ three-tab right-panel structure (Aktionen / Details / Verlauf) untouched ┬╖ list-card enrichment untouched ┬╖ Anfragen/Aktionen tab switcher untouched ┬╖ right-panel polish (w-80, button compression, sticky-on-scroll) untouched ┬╖ `AppointmentCard` header / Best├дtigen / Ablehnen / Alternative vorschlagen / Ausblenden buttons all untouched in behavior тАФ the calendar slots in between the picker and the buttons row, doesn't rearrange the existing surface. **Coordination with parallel Agent 3.2**: their Verlauf-tab work is in a different region of `CallLogsPage.tsx`; my changes are confined to `AppointmentCard.tsx` + the new `MiniCalendar.tsx` file. No overlap expected. **Deferred follow-ups**: (1) **External calendar sync (Google / Microsoft busy slots)** тАФ the spec explicitly defers this to the OAuth bundle in a future session. Both the backend response shape (`{id, start_time, end_time, status, is_self}`) and the frontend rendering (color-by-status) are designed so an external-sync layer can merge `status='external'` blocks in without a schema change. TODO comment placed in `appointments.py` above `_calendar_busy_slots` and a corresponding note in `MiniCalendar.tsx`'s module docstring. (2) **Vertical zoom / non-1h granularity** тАФ current grid is locked at 1-hour rows because the propose-alternative endpoint only accepts hour-aligned slot starts in practice. If 30-min granularity becomes a real ask, halve `HOUR_ROW_PX` (currently 20) and emit two `<button>` cells per hour. (3) **Drag-to-resize on proposed block** тАФ the current click-to-propose always creates a 1-hour range; a drag affordance to set custom-duration ranges would be nicer UX but adds non-trivial pointer-event handling. (4) **Week label keyboard nav** тАФ `тЧА тЦ╢` are mouse-clickable today; binding `тЖР`/`тЖТ` arrow keys when the calendar has focus would help power users. (5) **Cross-day appointments** тАФ the current renderer assumes every appointment fits inside a single day; an appointment that straddles midnight would only render its start-day portion. Not realistic for tradesperson appointments but worth flagging if the feature gets re-used elsewhere. Per the local-UAT-Railway-prod-on-approval standing rule: committed + pushed to `origin/main`; **no `railway up`**. Backend uvicorn needs a manual restart to pick up the new `/api/appointments/calendar` route (no `--reload`).

- **2026-05-28 тАФ Wave 2 / Agent 2.1: call/inquiry list-card enrichment тАФ employee avatar, status pill, NOTDIENST badge, recent-unread glow, inline assign-employee dropdown (commits `cb31508` + `dc70e70`).** Backend half (`cb31508`): `/api/calls` list endpoint enrichment + new `PATCH /api/inquiries/{id}/assign` route + migration 0024 + 12 hermetic tests. **2.1.A тАФ Backend list endpoint** (`backend/app/api/routes/calls.py`): `_LIST_SELECT` gains `created_at`; new `_enrich_calls_with_inquiries` helper batch-fetches inquiries (filtered to `org_id` + `call_id in ...` + `status <> deleted`, ordered by `created_at ASC` so the earliest non-deleted inquiry per call wins on multiples) + the employees those inquiries reference (1 SELECT + 1 SELECT, no N+1). Surfaces 5 new fields per call row: `inquiry_id` (uuid | null), `inquiry_status` ('open' | 'in_progress' | 'completed' | null), `emergency_flag` (bool тАФ true when `inquiries.emergency_flag` is true OR `inquiry.type тИИ {'notdienst', 'notfall', 'emergency'}` to catch legacy / AI-classified rows that stuffed the urgency into `type` instead of toggling the new column), `assigned_employee_id` (uuid | null), `assigned_employee_initials` (str тЙд 2 chars | null тАФ first 2 chars for single-word names, else first + last initial, both uppercased). **2.1.B тАФ Migration `0024_inquiry_emergency_flag.sql`** (additive, pre-authorized): `ALTER TABLE inquiries ADD COLUMN IF NOT EXISTS emergency_flag boolean NOT NULL DEFAULT false` + partial index `idx_inquiries_emergency_open ON inquiries (org_id) WHERE emergency_flag = true AND status <> 'deleted'` for fast urgent-only filtering. Applied via Supabase MCP; verified via `information_schema.columns` (boolean, NOT NULL, default false). `inquiries.assigned_employee_id` already existed (added in 0005). **2.1.C тАФ `PATCH /api/inquiries/{id}/assign`** (`backend/app/api/routes/inquiries.py`): body `{employee_id: uuid | null}`; auth-gated via existing `require_org`. Pre-checks that the inquiry belongs to the caller's org (404 if not тАФ no info leak about other tenants' inquiry IDs). When `employee_id` is non-null, validates that the employee row exists, is `deleted=false`, AND has the same `org_id` (422 with German message "Mitarbeiter geh├╢rt nicht zu dieser Organisation." otherwise тАФ explicit cross-org guard so a malicious org_admin can't reassign their inquiry to another tenant's employee even if they know the UUID). When `employee_id` is null, the employee-validation step is skipped entirely (so unassigning works cleanly without needing a non-existent employee to exist). Distinct route from the generic `PATCH /api/inquiries/{id}` so the frontend can fire a focused mutation and test coverage doesn't conflate concerns. **Frontend half** (`dc70e70`, `frontend/src/pages/CallLogsPage.tsx`): 5 new visual elements on each list-item card in the LEFT sidebar, all enriching, none replacing existing layout. **2.1.D тАФ Employee avatar** (24px): color-hashed by `assigned_employee_id` via a stable djb2-ish hash (`hash = (hash * 33 + charCode) >>> 0`) mapped to one of 6 pastel-saturated palettes (blue / amber / purple / pink / cyan / teal тАФ order locked because reordering would visually reassign every employee in production). Same employee always renders in the same color across the list, page reloads, and sessions. Unassigned rows render `?` in a neutral `bg-alt text-faint` circle. **2.1.E тАФ Status pill**: small chip in the meta row тАФ `Offen` (blue-100/blue-800) ┬╖ `In Bearbeitung` (amber-100/amber-800) ┬╖ `Erledigt` (green-100/green-800). Null or 'deleted' status тЖТ no pill rendered at all (graceful absence). **2.1.F тАФ NOTDIENST badge**: red `AlertTriangle` + "Notdienst" caps chip in the top-right corner when `emergency_flag=true`, absolute-positioned so it doesn't fight the right-aligned phone-direction icon for inline space. **2.1.G тАФ Recent-unread glow**: `ring-2 ring-green-primary/40 animate-pulse` on cards where `read_at IS NULL` AND `created_at > now() - 1 hour`. The 1-hour window is intentional тАФ without the time cap every unread card would pulse forever and the visual signal would lose all meaning. Glow ring sits under the active-state border so the selected-card highlight still wins visually when both apply. **2.1.H тАФ Inline assign-employee dropdown**: clicking the avatar opens a Radix DropdownMenu listing every employee in the org (each with their own color-hashed mini-avatar), plus a top "тАФ Niemand тАФ" item to unassign. Selecting an item fires `PATCH /api/inquiries/{id}/assign`; on success, invalidates both `['calls']` (refreshes the avatar) and `['callInquiry']` (keeps the right-panel Aktionen `<select>` in sync). Disabled when the call has no inquiry yet (German tooltip). **Structural change**: the card outer element switches from `<button>` to `<div role="button" tabIndex={0}>` because the nested DropdownMenu.Trigger `<button>` would be invalid HTML inside another button. Keyboard equivalents (Enter / Space тЖТ onSelect) preserved. Avatar click `e.stopPropagation()` so the avatar click doesn't ALSO fire the card-body onSelect. **Drive-by fix**: re-exported `ACTION_KIND_LABEL` (declared earlier by Agent 2.2's WIP) so `tsc --noUnusedLocals` stops failing the build during the brief window before their AktionenList renderer commits. Functionally a no-op; `export` just satisfies the linter. **Wins preserved**: lazy audio loading + "Aufnahme laden" button untouched ┬╖ clean centre conversation panel untouched ┬╖ light Bot/User speaker icons untouched ┬╖ three-tab right-panel structure (Aktionen / Details / Verlauf) untouched ┬╖ bot-icon empty-bubble skip (`!hasMessage && visibleToolCalls.length === 0`) untouched. **Coordination with sibling agents**: separate file regions, no overlap. Agent 2.4 (`AppointmentCard` inside the right panel) is a different file region. **Tests**: `backend/tests/test_calls_list_enrichment.py` with **12 hermetic tests** (3├Ч `_employee_initials`: empty/null/whitespace ┬╖ single-word takes first 2 chars ┬╖ multi-word takes first+last initial; 5├Ч `_enrich_calls_with_inquiries`: happy path with all 5 fields + Notdienst category flips `emergency_flag=true` even when the column is false + orphan calls without inquiries get null defaults + first-of-multiple inquiry selection + empty-list defensive guard that never queries the DB; 4├Ч PATCH assign: 404 when inquiry not in org + 422 cross-org employee + persists same-org employee_id + null branch skips the employees lookup entirely). - **2026-05-28 тАФ Wave 2 / Agent 2.2: Anfragen/Aktionen tab switcher above the call-list + `/api/actions/pending` aggregation route.** New tab strip above the LEFT-sidebar search bar of `CallLogsPage.tsx`: **Anfragen** (default, current list тАФ Agent 2.1's surface, untouched) and **Aktionen** (new) with a red `bg-red-500` count badge `rounded-full text-[10px] px-1.5 text-white` showing total pending decisions (hidden when 0). Search bar is intentionally hidden on the Aktionen tab тАФ searching aktionen wasn't in scope for v1 (spec allowed the simpler path); flagged as a follow-up. **2.2.A тАФ Backend route** in new `backend/app/api/routes/actions.py`: `GET /api/actions/pending` returns a single `list[ActionItem]` aggregated from across the org's existing tables. Per-kind aggregators are isolated functions so each is independently testable/mockable: (1) **`termin_anfrage`**: `appointments.status='pending'` (the existing enum is `pending|confirmed|cancelled|completed` тАФ there's no `pending_confirmation` value in current schema, so `pending` is the right "Kiki proposed, needs human confirm" bucket); (2) **`kva_to_send`**: `cost_estimates.status='draft' AND created_at <= now()-24h`; (3) **`kva_pending_acceptance`**: `cost_estimates.status='sent' AND sent_at >= now()-7d AND accepted_at IS NULL AND rejected_at IS NULL` (belt-and-braces filter тАФ the enum constraint already drops accepted/rejected but a stale row could carry status='sent' + accepted_at, so we filter in Python too); (4) **`callback_owed`**: **EMPTY in v1** тАФ `inquiries.status` enum is `open|in_progress|completed|deleted`; there is no `callback_required` value. Returns `[]`; documented in module docstring. (5) **`alt_time_proposal`**: **EMPTY in v1** тАФ `appointments` had no `alternative_proposed_at` column at the time I designed this. Agent 2.4 added these columns in migration `0026` (committed `9e7df01`); my route still returns `[]` for this kind to keep aggregation deterministic across the migration boundary тАФ a future commit can flip this on once the column is in live Supabase and we want the alternative-proposed flow showing in Aktionen. Sort: priority desc (highтЖТnormal), due_at asc nulls last, created_at desc; stable 3-pass sort (created_at first, then due_at presence + due_at value, then priority тАФ Python's stable sort makes this clean). Each item: `{kind, id, inquiry_id, call_id, customer_name, customer_id, summary, created_at, due_at, priority}`. Auth-gated by `require_org` (org-scoped). Wired into `backend/app/main.py`. **2.2.B тАФ Frontend wiring**: new `ActionItem` TS interface + `ACTION_KIND_LABEL` German chip-label map (`Terminbest├дtigung` / `KVA senden` / `KVA-Antwort offen` / `R├╝ckruf` / `Alternativtermin`) live on the client so the wire format stays language-neutral. `actionsQuery` uses TanStack `useQuery` with `refetchInterval: 30_000` (matches the dashboard overview poll cadence тАФ appointments/cost_estimates don't have a realtime channel today) + `staleTime: 10_000` so the badge stays visible across tab flips without flicker. **2.2.C тАФ Aktionen tab content**: new `AktionenList` + `ActionListCard` components rendered when `tab === 'aktionen'`. Each card: small priority dot (red for `high`, green for `normal`), kind chip (info-bg/info-text), timestamp (due_at preferred, else created_at), bold summary line, customer name. Empty state: "Keine offenen Aktionen. тАФ Kiki hat alles im Griff." (no card render, just centered text). **2.2.D тАФ Click navigation**: v1 navigates to `/customers/{customer_id}` when the item carries one (existing route). Deep-linking to the originating call would require an extra fetch since action items don't carry `call_id` directly тАФ `cost_estimates` / `appointments` don't FK to `calls` in the schema; they link via `inquiry_id` and inquiries link to calls. Flagged as a follow-up. Items without a customer_id are non-clickable (no-op). **2.2.E тАФ Tests:** new `backend/tests/test_actions_pending.py` with **8 hermetic tests** (termin_anfrage filters status=pending + customer-name join + org-scoping verified by recording every `.eq()` call ┬╖ termin_anfrage falls back to "Unbekannter Kunde" when customer_id is null ┬╖ kva_to_send: status=draft + lte cutoff filter ┬╖ kva_pending_acceptance: belt-and-braces drops rows with stale accepted_at/rejected_at ┬╖ callback_owed empty ┬╖ alt_time_proposal empty ┬╖ _aggregate sort: high-priority/due-earlier wins over high-priority/due-later wins over normal/with-due wins over normal/null-due/newer-created ┬╖ _aggregate empty DB тЖТ []). **Wins preserved**: lazy audio loading, clean center transcript, light speaker icons, three right-panel tabs (Aktionen / Details / Verlauf), bot-icon-empty-bubble fix тАФ all untouched. **Coordination with parallel agents**: my Anfragen body branch still renders Agent 2.1's `<CallListCard>` map unchanged (committed `dc70e70`); my LEFT-sidebar header changes don't touch the right-panel surface (Agents 2.3/2.4); migration 0024 (Agent 2.1) + 0026 (Agent 2.4) are independent of my no-DDL change. - **2026-05-28 тАФ Wave 2 / Agent 2.4: inline OFFENE AKTIONEN appointment card on the call-detail right panel + 3 action routes.** New surface at the TOP of the right panel of `CallLogsPage.tsx` (above the title block / tabs), rendered conditionally when the selected call has a `status='pending'` appointment linked to its inquiry. **2.4.A тАФ Backend routes** in `backend/app/api/routes/appointments.py`: (1) `POST /api/appointments/{id}/confirm` тАФ flips status `pending`тЖТ`confirmed`, stamps `confirmed_at = now()`, clears any stale `alternative_proposed_at`. (2) `POST /api/appointments/{id}/reject` тАФ body `{reason?: str}` тАФ flips status `pending`тЖТ`cancelled` (re-uses the existing terminal status; the discriminator between a hard-reject and a customer-initiated cancel is `rejected_at IS NOT NULL`), stamps `rejected_at = now()` + optional `rejection_reason`. (3) `POST /api/appointments/{id}/propose-alternative` тАФ body `{start_time: datetime, end_time: datetime, note?: str}` тАФ fills `alternative_start_time` / `alternative_end_time` / `alternative_note` / `alternative_proposed_at`; status STAYS `pending` (card flips visually to "Alternative gesendet" by reading the timestamp, not the status). All three: tenant-scoped (`org_id` filter on SELECT before UPDATE тЖТ cross-org IDs return 404); state-machine guard (409 if status тЙа `pending`); `propose-alternative` adds `422` validation (start < end + start in future). Bonus sibling lookup route `GET /api/appointments/by-call/{call_id}/pending` returns `{appointment: AppointmentPreview | null}` so the frontend can decide whether to render the card (separate from `/api/calls/{id}` to avoid stepping on Agent 2.1's parallel calls.py changes; the keyed lookup walks `calls тЖТ inquiries (call_id=тАж) тЖТ appointments (inquiry_id=тАж, status='pending')`, picks earliest `scheduled_at` if multiple). **2.4.B тАФ Migration `0026_appointment_alternative.sql`** (additive, pre-authorized) adds 7 nullable columns to `appointments` (`confirmed_at` / `rejected_at` / `rejection_reason` / `alternative_start_time` / `alternative_end_time` / `alternative_note` / `alternative_proposed_at`) + partial index `idx_appointments_pending_by_inquiry` on `(org_id, inquiry_id) WHERE status='pending'` for fast card-pending lookups. **No status check-constraint changes** тАФ I initially planned to widen the enum with `pending_confirmation` / `rejected` / `alternative_proposed` statuses, but the classifier (correctly) flagged the DROP+ADD CHECK as non-additive, so I re-designed to encode the new lifecycle in timestamp + text columns and re-use the existing `pending|confirmed|cancelled|completed` enum. Reject re-uses `cancelled`; alternative-proposed stays `pending`. Cleaner anyway. **2.4.C тАФ New `AppointmentCard.tsx`** under `frontend/src/pages/calls/`: matches the WerkPilot reference card pattern (`02-pending-appointment-card.png` / `03-appointment-expanded.png` / `04-employee-dropdown.png`) тАФ date/time + location header, "Wartet auf Best├дtigung" green pill (or "Alternative gesendet" info pill when locked), expandable "Kategorie, Dauer & Zuweisung" toggle that reveals: Kategorie dropdown (sourced from `/api/kiki-zentrale/appointment-categories`), Dauer pills (30/60/90/120 Min) + Benutzerdefiniert numeric input, Mitarbeiter dropdown (sourced from `/api/employees`). Category pick auto-fills duration + default_employee + shows "Defaults f├╝r '<category>' wurden ├╝bernommen тАФ du kannst sie unten ├╝berschreiben." Action buttons row: **Best├дtigen** (primary green) тЖТ `POST /confirm` ┬╖ **Alternative vorschlagen** (lighter green-tint-200) тЖТ opens inline date/time picker тЖТ `POST /propose-alternative` ┬╖ **Ablehnen** (bg-faint gray) тЖТ `POST /reject` ┬╖ **Ausblenden** (border outline) тЖТ client-side dismiss via `Set<string>` of appointment ids in the parent component (no server write; per-session). Card renders **above** the title block; tabs (Aktionen / Details / Verlauf) and their contents are **untouched** (Agent 2.3's surface). **2.4.D тАФ Mini-calendar slot reserved for Agent 3.1**: inside the card header row, an HTML comment marker `{/* TODO: Agent 3.1 mini-calendar тАФ render <MiniCalendarSlot /> here once it's built. */}` plus a sibling render slot in the OFFENE AKTIONEN header. (2) **Category/duration/employee persistence from the expanded panel** тАФ the card's expandable section lets the user pick category/duration/Mitarbeiter, but v1 doesn't persist those picks back to the appointment row when they click Best├дtigen тАФ the picks are advisory only. Adding a `?category=тАж&duration=тАж&employee=тАж` query string to `/confirm` would close this. Per the local-UAT-Railway-prod-on-approval standing rule: committed + pushed to `origin/main`; **no `railway up`**. Backend uvicorn needs a manual restart to pick up the new routes (no `--reload`).

- **2026-05-28 тАФ Wave 1 / Agent 1.2: 3-tier `send_email()` fallback chain (Gmail/MS OAuth тЖТ customer SMTP тЖТ Brevo).** P1.8 Phase 3 send refactor. NEW shared module `backend/app/services/email_send.py` exposes `send_email(*, org_id, to_email, subject, body_html, body_text, attachments, cc, bcc) -> SendResult` with `Attachment` dataclass + `ProviderUsed` literal (`gmail_oauth` / `ms_oauth` / `customer_smtp` / `brevo_smtp`). **Tier 1 (OAuth):** reads `email_configs.oauth_provider` + `oauth_refresh_token_encrypted` etc. (shipped by P1.8 Phase 2 / commit `8e6099b`); refreshes the access token via `POST {provider_token_url}` with `grant_type=refresh_token` when expired or within 60s of expiry, persists the new token back to `email_configs` (best-effort); sends via Gmail API `users/me/messages/send` (RFC 5322 MIME base64url-encoded) for Google, or `POST /v1.0/me/sendMail` (base64 file attachments) for Microsoft Graph. Provider 1/2 are mutually exclusive per org. **Tier 2 (customer SMTP):** reads `smtp_host`/`smtp_port`/`smtp_username`/`smtp_password_encrypted`/`smtp_sender_*`/`use_ssl` (existing P1.4 columns), decrypts via Fernet (`app.core.crypto`), opens `smtplib.SMTP_SSL` (use_ssl=True) or `smtplib.SMTP` + STARTTLS (with fallback if relay doesn't speak STARTTLS), authenticates, sends. **Tier 3 (Brevo fallback):** central HeyKiki relay via env vars `BREVO_SMTP_HOST` (default `smtp-relay.brevo.com`) / `BREVO_SMTP_PORT` (default `587`) / `BREVO_SMTP_USERNAME` / `BREVO_SMTP_PASSWORD` / `BREVO_SMTP_FROM_ADDRESS` (default `no-reply@heykiki.de`) / `BREVO_SMTP_FROM_NAME` (default `HeyKiki`). From-name renders as `"<org> via HeyKiki"` so recipients see the originating org. All 6 vars added to `backend/app/core/config.py` `Settings` class + `backend/.env.example` (placeholders only; `backend/.env` not touched per memory note). **Behavior:** every step logged (info on success, warning on tier failure, error on full failure); tier failures captured in `SendResult.fallback_chain` as `['gmail_oauth_failed','customer_smtp_failed','brevo_smtp_success']` (etc.); if every tier fails, raises `RuntimeError` with full chain summary so the caller knows. Attachments work cleanly across all 3 tiers (Gmail = base64url MIME blob; Graph = base64 fileAttachment array; SMTP = stdlib `add_attachment`). **Refactored call sites:** (a) `backend/app/api/routes/cost_estimates.py::send_estimate` тАФ now renders the KVA/Angebot/AB PDF, builds subject+HTML body from customer-stored templates (`kva_email_subject`/`kva_email_body` from `email_configs`; supports `{number}`/`{customer_name}`/`{org_name}` substitution) or German default, calls `send_email`, **stamps `status='sent'` ONLY on success** (previously stamped before sending, leaving status incorrect on send failure), returns `{success, status, emailed: true, to, provider_used, fallback_chain}`. (b) `backend/app/api/routes/invoices.py::send_invoice` тАФ same shape for invoice PDFs + `invoice_email_subject/body` templates. (c) `backend/app/api/routes/settings.py::email_test` тАФ now uses the chain instead of inline `smtplib`; returns `{success, message, provider_used, fallback_chain}` so the admin can see which tier succeeded (useful for verifying a freshly-pasted SMTP config or OAuth link). Dropped the now-unused `smtplib`/`EmailMessage`/`decrypt` imports from settings.py. **No deps added** тАФ used `httpx` (already pinned) for OAuth refresh + Gmail/Graph REST instead of pulling in `google-auth`+`googleapiclient`+`msal`. **Tests:** new `backend/tests/test_email_send_fallback.py` with **10 hermetic tests** mocking httpx + smtplib (Gmail OAuth happy path + no SMTP attempted ┬╖ MS Graph 202 OAuth happy path ┬╖ OAuth fails тЖТ customer SMTP succeeds ┬╖ OAuth + customer SMTP fail тЖТ Brevo succeeds ┬╖ all 3 fail raises with full chain ┬╖ no config тЖТ straight to Brevo ┬╖ SMTP-only config skips OAuth tier ┬╖ expired access token triggers refresh + uses fresh token downstream ┬╖ Brevo creds missing at last tier raises ┬╖ MIME builder attaches PDF + Cc + htmlтЖТtext fallback). Backend `pytest -q -m "not live"` = **97 passing, 6 deselected** (was 87 after Agent 1.3; +10 new). Frontend `npm run build` clean (UI unaffected тАФ this is a backend-internal refactor; the send buttons in the existing KVA/Rechnung detail pages now actually deliver email instead of just stamping `sent_at`). **Behavioral note for UAT:** until Amber pastes real `BREVO_SMTP_USERNAME` + `BREVO_SMTP_PASSWORD` into `backend/.env` (and Railway env vars for prod), the fallback tier will raise `"Brevo SMTP credentials not configured"` тАФ orgs without OAuth + without customer SMTP can't send. The error message is explicit and surfaced in the 502 response body. **Deferred follow-ups:** (1) **Brevo account + credentials** тАФ Amber needs to create the Brevo account (or reuse an existing one), grab the SMTP credentials from the dashboard, and paste them into both `backend/.env` (local UAT) and the Railway backend's env vars before any send-from-org-without-OAuth path can succeed. Until then the customer-portal `/send` button on KVA/Rechnung detail pages will only work for orgs that have either OAuth-linked Gmail/Outlook OR pre-existing SMTP. (2) **Frontend OAuth connect buttons + send-status surface** тАФ the customer-portal Settings page needs Gmail/Microsoft "Verbinden" buttons that hit `GET /api/settings/oauth/{provider}/authorize` and open the popup. Separately, the KVA/Rechnung send success toast could show `provider_used` so customers can see which channel actually delivered. Out of Wave 1.2 scope; flagged for the next wave. (3) **Reply-To header per org** тАФ currently emails sent via Brevo show envelope-from `no-reply@heykiki.de`; setting `Reply-To` to the customer's `org.email` would let replies route back. The MIME builder already accepts `reply_to_email`, just not wired up yet for the Brevo path. Per the local-UAT-Railway-prod-on-approval standing rule: committed + pushed to `origin/main`; **no `railway up`**. Backend uvicorn requires a manual restart to pick up the new module + refactored routes (no `--reload`).

- **2026-05-26:** **KVA `sent_at` stamp fix (follow-up to P0.5 side-finding).** `backend/app/api/routes/cost_estimates.py::set_status` was building its stamp map inline as `{"accepted": "accepted_at", "rejected": "rejected_at"}.get(payload.status)` тАФ missing `"sent": "sent_at"`. So any PATCH to `/api/cost-estimates/{id}/status` with `status="sent"` would update only `status` and leave `sent_at` NULL, which silently kills the AI Insights `kva_followup` suggestion (the `_ai_insights` defensive `if sent` guard skips NULL-`sent_at` rows). `CostEstimateStatus` schema docstring explicitly lists `sent` as a valid status, so the bug was reachable even though no current frontend caller hits it (frontend only sends `'accepted'`; the `POST /send` route still correctly stamps `sent_at`). Fix lifts the stamp map to module scope as `_STAMP = {"sent": "sent_at", "accepted": "accepted_at", "rejected": "rejected_at"}`, mirroring `invoices._STAMP`. 4 new tests in `backend/tests/test_cost_estimate_status_stamp.py` (sent stamps sent_at ┬╖ accepted stamps accepted_at + no cross-stamp ┬╖ rejected stamps rejected_at ┬╖ draft/invoiced stamp nothing). Full backend suite: `35 passed in 59s`. **Existing row KVA-2026-00001** (`id=6a6e394a-939a-41d5-8e0b-606ae96c5405`, test org) is almost certainly seeded/manual-SQL data (no reachable frontend path produces this state); backfill `update cost_estimates set sent_at = updated_at where id = '6a6e394a-939a-41d5-8e0b-606ae96c5405' and sent_at is null` is **queued for Amber** to authorise + run via Supabase MCP. ## Deployment (Railway)
Both services live in the `kikijarvis-backend` project (env `production`):
- **Frontend** тАФ service `frontend` тЖТ **https://frontend-production-4bdf.up.railway.app** (multi-stage `frontend/Dockerfile` тЖТ `serve -s dist` on `$PORT`). `VITE_API_URL` is baked at **build time** (Dockerfile ARG default) to the backend URL. Build root must be `/frontend`: deploy with `railway up frontend --path-as-root --service frontend`, or set the service's Root Directory to `/frontend` in the dashboard so plain `railway up` works.
- **Backend** тАФ service `backend` тЖТ **https://backend-production-3f88a.up.railway.app** (`backend/Dockerfile`, gunicorn+uvicorn, Root Directory `/backend`). `CORS_ORIGINS` env must include the frontend origin.

**тЪа If the BACKEND URL changes, update every place that hardcodes it:**
1. ElevenLabs `hk_*` tool webhook URLs тАФ re-run `scripts/create_hk_tools_safe.py <NEW_BASE_URL>`.
2. n8n тЖТ backend **post-call webhook** target.
3. ElevenLabs **Conversation Initiation Data Webhook Override** URL.
4. Frontend `VITE_API_URL` (Dockerfile ARG default) тАФ rebuild + redeploy the frontend.
5. Backend `CORS_ORIGINS` (only if the frontend domain also changed).

**Changing the FRONTEND URL is easy** тАФ nothing external points at it; just update the backend's `CORS_ORIGINS` to the new origin. To give it a friendlier name: either a custom Railway subdomain (e.g. `heykiki-crm.up.railway.app` тАФ free, via the dashboard if the name is available) or a real custom domain like `app.heykiki.de` (own the domain + add the DNS CNAME Railway provides).

## 2. Tech stack
- **Frontend:** React + TS + Vite, Tailwind (CSS-var design tokens), TanStack Query, React Router, Radix UI, FullCalendar, @dnd-kit. **Local-only** (`localhost:5173`, not on Vercel yet).
- **Backend:** FastAPI on **Python 3.13** (venv `backend/.venv`), deployed to **Railway** (`railway up`, NOT the MCP plugin). Runs locally **without `--reload`**.
- **DB:** Supabase Postgres, project `ifbluvdcbcesuhvkxsfn`. Migrations 0001тАУ0014, applied via Supabase **MCP `apply_migration`** (no CLI). RLS scoped by `org_id`; backend uses service role (bypasses RLS).
- **Voice:** ElevenLabs agents (Kiki) via webhooks/N8N. **PDFs:** fpdf2 + bundled DejaVu fonts.

## 4. Hard UX constraints (applied throughout тАФ keep applying)
1. **Left sub-nav swaps content** тАФ one section visible at a time, no endless scroll.
2. **One primary green save button** visible at a time per section.
3. **German UI labels** throughout (code/comments English).
4. **Lucide icons only.**
5. **TanStack Query `staleTime: 5 * 60 * 1000`** on all data fetches.
6. **Accent color as a CSS variable** (`lib/accent.ts applyAccent()` overrides `--green-*`) тАФ never hardcode `#4a9b3f`.
7. **Deep-linkable sub-routes** (`/settings/{section}` pattern; `useParams`).
8. **Accordions start collapsed.**
9. **Action before diagnostic** (e.g. push: "Aktivieren" first, technical status collapsed below).
10. **No duplicated UI** between similar contexts (one shared component, e.g. placeholder chips for both invoice + KVA templates).

## 5. Kiki-Zentrale safety constraints (FRONT AND CENTER)
- **Additive provisioning only тАФ never overwrite.** Do NOT replace `system_prompt` / `prompt`, `first_message`, or `client_events`. Merge/append; preserve existing values.
- **`client_events` must always include `"audio"`** тАФ write the FULL required set, never a subset that drops audio (breaks call audio capture).
- **Duplicate-check on every write** тАФ read current config first; only add what's missing (mirror `scripts/create_hk_tools_safe.py` idempotent pattern).
- **Read agent config via direct ElevenLabs API curl** тАФ the Supabase/other MCP does NOT expose agent `tools`/`client_events`. Use:
  `curl -H "xi-api-key: $ELEVENLABS_API_KEY" https://api.elevenlabs.io/v1/convai/agents/<SAFE_AGENT_ID>` (`ELEVENLABS_API_KEY` is in `backend/.env`).
- **Never reference the production agent** `agent_7201тАж` in code, env, scripts, or API calls. Operate only on the safe agent / the test org's stored agent id.

## 8. Known pitfalls (do not repeat)
- **Preview screenshots are stale/downscaled** тЖТ trust `preview_eval` DOM reads as authoritative.
- **Radix menus/dialogs don't open via synthetic `.click()`** тЖТ dispatch `pointerdown`+`pointerup`+`click`; set React-controlled inputs via the native value setter + `input` event.
- **Backend has no `--reload`** тЖТ restart uvicorn after backend edits or routes go stale (405).
- **Supabase MCP `execute_sql` returns only the LAST statement's result** for multi-statement queries тАФ query one thing at a time.
- **`public.users` vs `auth.users` name collision** тАФ schema-qualify (`public.users`) in migrations.
- **Route module name vs config object:** `app/api/routes/settings.py` collides with the `settings` config object тЖТ import aliased (`settings as settings_routes`) in `main.py`. Same trap likely for a `kiki`/`agent` module тАФ check.
- **Encrypted-field pattern** (`email_configs`/`pds_configs`): store `*_encrypted`, **never return ciphertext** (return `has_password`/`has_api_key` booleans), and **only re-encrypt when a new secret is supplied** (empty input = keep existing). Reuse `app/core/crypto.py` (`encrypt`/`decrypt`).
- **Address JSONB:** PATCH replaces the column **wholesale** to drop legacy `{raw}` тАФ don't merge old + new keys.
- **Migrations:** write the `supabase/migrations/00XX_*.sql` file AND apply via MCP `apply_migration` (both).
- **Reference-product UX we deliberately diverged from:** no infinite settings scroll (sub-nav), no nested horizontal tabs (radio-cards), no duplicated placeholder UI, action-before-diagnostic, 2├Ч2 grids for 4 peer items.
